<p><b>Luka Modri</b> (<small>Croatian pronunciation:&#160;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Serbo-Croatian" title="Help:IPA/Serbo-Croatian">[lûka mdrit]</a></span>;<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> born 9 September 1985) is a Croatian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielder</a> for Spanish club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captains</a> the <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia national team</a>. He plays mainly as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, but can also play as an <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> or as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>, usually deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Playmaker#Deep-lying_playmakers" title="Playmaker">deep-lying playmaker</a>. He is widely regarded as one of the best midfielders of his generation,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;nb 1&#93;</a></sup> and the greatest Croatian footballer of all-time.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;nb 2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Zadar" title="Zadar">Zadar</a>, Modri's childhood coincided with the <a href="/wiki/Croatian_War_of_Independence" title="Croatian War of Independence">Croatian War of Independence</a> which displaced his family. In 2002, he was signed by <a href="/wiki/GNK_Dinamo_Zagreb" title="GNK Dinamo Zagreb">Dinamo Zagreb</a> at age 16, after showing promise with his hometown club <a href="/wiki/NK_Zadar" title="NK Zadar">NK Zadar</a>'s youth team. He continued his development in Zagreb, before spells on loan to <a href="/wiki/H%C5%A0K_Zrinjski_Mostar" title="HŠK Zrinjski Mostar">Zrinjski Mostar</a> and <a href="/wiki/NK_Inter_Zapre%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="NK Inter Zapreši">Inter Zapreši</a>. He made his debut for Dinamo in 2005 and won three consecutive league titles and domestic cups, being named the <a href="/wiki/Prva_HNL_Player_of_the_Year" title="Prva HNL Player of the Year">Prva HNL Player of the Year</a> in 2007. In 2008, he moved to <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> for a <a href="/wiki/List_of_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._records_and_statistics#Transfers" title="List of Tottenham Hotspur F.C. records and statistics">club-record transfer fee</a> of £16.5&#160;million, where he led Spurs to their first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> appearance in almost 50 years, reaching the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Quarter-finals" title="2010–11 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">quarter-finals</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2010–11 UEFA Champions League">2010–11 tournament</a>.
</p><p>In the summer of 2012, Modri joined Real Madrid for a £30&#160;million transfer fee. There he became a key contributor and helped the team win <i><a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF#La_Décima_and_European_treble" title="Real Madrid CF">La Décima</a></i> and was selected for the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">2013–14 Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League#Squad_of_the_season" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">squad of the season</a>. After <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> took over Madrid, Modri was critical to three consecutive Champions League titles from <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16</a> to <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18</a>, each time being voted into the squad of the season. He has won 17 major trophies at Real Madrid including four <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> titles, two <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> titles, one <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> and three <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cup</a> titles. He won the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga_Awards" title="La Liga Awards">La Liga Award</a> for "Best Midfielder" in 2016 for the second time, and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Football_Awards#Best_Midfielder" title="UEFA Club Football Awards">UEFA Club Football Award</a> for "Best Midfielder" in 2017 and 2018. In 2015, he became the first Croatian player to be included in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>, in which he was regularly included until 2019, as well in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> between 2016 and 2018. In 2018, Modri became the first Croatian player to win the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Men%27s_Player_of_the_Year_Award" title="UEFA Men&#39;s Player of the Year Award">UEFA Men's Player of the Year Award</a>, and by winning <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Men%27s_Player" title="The Best FIFA Men&#39;s Player">The Best FIFA Men's Player</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a> awards, he became the first player other than <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> or <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> to claim the awards in more than a decade. In 2019, he was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Foot" title="Golden Foot">Golden Foot</a> award for career results and personality.
</p><p>Modri made his international debut for Croatia against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> in March 2006, and scored his first international goal in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>. He has since anchored Croatia's "<a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team#Dali&#39;s_second_&quot;golden_generation&quot;_(2017–present)" title="Croatia national football team">second Golden Generation</a>", participating in every major tournament Croatia has qualified for, including the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Euro 2008</a>, <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">2012</a>, and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">2016</a>, as well the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006</a>, <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014</a>, and <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>. At UEFA Euro 2008, he was selected for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008#UEFA_Team_of_the_Tournament" title="UEFA Euro 2008">Team of the Tournament</a>, becoming only the second Croatian to ever achieve this honour. Following group stage eliminations in his first two World Cups, Modri led Croatia to the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">2018 World Cup Final</a>, and he received the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Ball_(FIFA_World_Cup)" class="mw-redirect" title="Golden Ball (FIFA World Cup)">Golden Ball</a> award for Best Player of the Tournament. Furthermore, he has been named the <a href="/wiki/Croatian_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="Croatian Footballer of the Year">Croatian Footballer of the Year</a> a record eight times between 2007–2019.<sup id="cite_ref-CFY19_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CFY19-8">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Zadar_(20069585463).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Zadar_%2820069585463%29.jpg/220px-Zadar_%2820069585463%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Zadar_%2820069585463%29.jpg/330px-Zadar_%2820069585463%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Zadar_%2820069585463%29.jpg/440px-Zadar_%2820069585463%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4608" data-file-height="3072" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Zadar_(20069585463).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri was born in <a href="/wiki/Zadar" title="Zadar">Zadar</a>, Croatia where he began his youth career at <a href="/wiki/NK_Zadar" title="NK Zadar">NK Zadar</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Luka Modri was born on 9 September 1985 and was raised in the hamlet of Modrii which is a part of <a href="/wiki/Zaton_Obrova%C4%8Dki" title="Zaton Obrovaki">Zaton Obrovaki</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201620_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201620-9">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEop201415_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEop201415-10">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> a village situated on the southern slopes of the mountain <a href="/wiki/Velebit" title="Velebit">Velebit</a>, north of the city of <a href="/wiki/Zadar" title="Zadar">Zadar</a> in <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Republic_of_Croatia" title="Socialist Republic of Croatia">SR Croatia</a>, then a republic within <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Federal_Republic_of_Yugoslavia" title="Socialist Federal Republic of Yugoslavia">SFR Yugoslavia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He is the oldest child of Stipe Modri from Modrii and Radojka Dopu from <a href="/wiki/Kru%C5%A1evo,_Zadar_County" title="Kruševo, Zadar County">Kruševo</a> near <a href="/wiki/Obrovac,_Croatia" title="Obrovac, Croatia">Obrovac</a>, both of whom initially worked in a knitwear factory.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201617,_20,_22_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201617,_20,_22-14">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Nacional_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nacional-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Modri mostly spent his early years in the stone house of his paternal grandfather after whom he was named,<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201620_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201620-9">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEop201416_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEop201416-18">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> located on the road above the hamlet of Modrii,<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEModriMatteoni20205–6_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEModriMatteoni20205–6-19">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and was shepherding goats as a five-year-old.<sup id="cite_ref-ElvirUEFA_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ElvirUEFA-22">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, his childhood coincided with the <a href="/wiki/Croatian_War_of_Independence" title="Croatian War of Independence">Croatian War of Independence</a>—in 1991, when the war escalated, his family were forced to flee the area.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Modri's grandfather Luka was executed by <a href="/wiki/Log_Revolution" title="Log Revolution">Serb rebels</a> who were part of the police of <a href="/wiki/SAO_Krajina" title="SAO Krajina">SAO Krajina</a> in December 1991 near his house in Modrii,<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> and after the family fled the house was burned to the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201621–22_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201621–22-27">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Modri became a refugee and lived with his family in the Hotel Kolovare for seven years; he later moved to the Hotel Iž, both in Zadar.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Boboska_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Boboska-29">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MarcaBio2017_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcaBio2017-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> His father joined the <a href="/wiki/Croatian_Army" title="Croatian Army">Croatian Army</a> as an aeromechanic.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201622_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201622-31">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> In those years, thousands of bombs <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Zadar" title="Battle of Zadar">fell on the city</a> and football was a way to escape the reality of war.<sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He recalls it as a tough time for his family and something which shaped him as a person.<sup id="cite_ref-Nathanson_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nathanson-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AlanSmith_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlanSmith-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BoyMarca_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BoyMarca-34">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> He also said he was mostly unaware of the war because he befriended many other children and their parents did not let it affect their childhood.<sup id="cite_ref-Nacional_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nacional-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In these difficult circumstances, Modri began playing football, mostly at the hotel parking lot.<sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In 1992, he simultaneously entered the primary school and a sporting academy, the latter paid for with the little money the family had, sometimes helped by Modri's uncle.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Boboska_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Boboska-29">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Nacional_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nacional-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> As a boy he was inspired to play football by <a href="/wiki/Zvonimir_Boban" title="Zvonimir Boban">Zvonimir Boban</a> and <a href="/wiki/Francesco_Totti" title="Francesco Totti">Francesco Totti</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_years">Early years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Early years">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="1990s.E2.80.9305:_NK_Zadar_and_development_through_loans"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1990s–05:_NK_Zadar_and_development_through_loans">1990s–05: NK Zadar and development through loans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: 1990s–05: NK Zadar and development through loans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Supported by his family, he participated in representative camps and trained in <a href="/wiki/NK_Zadar" title="NK Zadar">NK Zadar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Nacional_16-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nacional-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He was under tutelage of coach Domagoj Baši and the head of the youth academy, Tomislav Baši.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Tomislav Baši, considered by Modri as his "sporting father",<sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MarcaBio2017_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcaBio2017-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> said Modri's father made him wooden shin guards because they had little money.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Nathanson_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nathanson-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BoyMarca_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BoyMarca-34">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> However, Modri later denied the story.<sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Due to being considered too young and light, he was not signed by Croatian powerhouse <a href="/wiki/HNK_Hajduk_Split" title="HNK Hajduk Split">Hajduk Split</a>, the most representative football club in the region of <a href="/wiki/Dalmatia" title="Dalmatia">Dalmatia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Nacional_16-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nacional-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> After displaying some talent, including at youth tournament in Italy,<sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Tomislav Baši arranged Modri's move to <a href="/wiki/GNK_Dinamo_Zagreb" title="GNK Dinamo Zagreb">Dinamo Zagreb</a> when Modri was a 16-year-old in late 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> After a season with Dinamo Zagreb's youth side, Modri was loaned in 2003 to <a href="/wiki/H%C5%A0K_Zrinjski_Mostar" title="HŠK Zrinjski Mostar">Zrinjski Mostar</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_of_Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Premier League of Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnian Premier League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Stvaran_11-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stvaran-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> During this period, he established his versatile style of play and became the Bosnian Premier League Player of the Year at only the age of 18.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Modri later said, "Someone who can play in the Bosnian Premier League can play anywhere," referring to its physical nature.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> The following year, he was loaned to Croatian side <a href="/wiki/NK_Inter_Zapre%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="NK Inter Zapreši">Inter Zapreši</a>. He spent one season there, helping the team to achieve second position in the <a href="/wiki/2004%E2%80%9305_Croatian_First_Football_League" title="2004–05 Croatian First Football League">Prva HNL</a><sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> and a place in the preliminary round of the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_UEFA_Cup" title="2005–06 UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a>. He also won the <a href="/wiki/Croatian_Footballer_of_the_Year#Croatian_Footballer_of_the_Year_(1991–present)" title="Croatian Footballer of the Year">Croatian Football Hope of the Year</a> award in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> He returned to Dinamo Zagreb in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dinamo_Zagreb">Dinamo Zagreb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Dinamo Zagreb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2005.E2.80.9308:_Breakthrough_in_Croatia"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2005–08:_Breakthrough_in_Croatia">2005–08: Breakthrough in Croatia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2005–08: Breakthrough in Croatia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_Croatian_First_Football_League" title="2005–06 Croatian First Football League">2005–06 season</a>, Modri signed a ten-year contract (his first long-term contract) with Dinamo Zagreb.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> With the contract's earnings, he bought a flat in Zadar for his family.<sup id="cite_ref-Holiga2012_13-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Holiga2012-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He secured a place in Dinamo's first team, contributing 7 goals in 31 matches to help win the league.<sup id="cite_ref-NFT_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NFT-40">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_NK_Dinamo_Zagreb_season" title="2006–07 NK Dinamo Zagreb season">2006–07 season</a>, Dinamo again won the league, with Modri making a similar contribution.<sup id="cite_ref-NFT_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NFT-40">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He was the main provider for striker <a href="/wiki/Eduardo_da_Silva" title="Eduardo da Silva">Eduardo</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> which helped Modri win the <a href="/wiki/Prva_HNL_Player_of_the_Year_(Tportal)" title="Prva HNL Player of the Year (Tportal)">Prva HNL Player of the Year</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-Real_Profile_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Real_Profile-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> The following season, Modri as a team captain,<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> led Dinamo's attempt to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_UEFA_Cup" title="2007–08 UEFA Cup">2007–08 UEFA Cup</a>. In the final play-off stage, Modri converted a penalty in the second and away fixture against <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>; the match finished 1–1 after regular time. Dinamo won the match and play-off with a score of 3–2 after <a href="/wiki/Overtime_(sports)" title="Overtime (sports)">extra time</a> with two goals from teammate <a href="/wiki/Mario_Mand%C5%BEuki%C4%87" title="Mario Mandžuki">Mario Mandžuki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> However, Dinamo Zagreb failed to advance beyond the group stage. In his last home match with the club at <a href="/wiki/Maksimir_Stadium" class="mw-redirect" title="Maksimir Stadium">Maksimir Stadium</a>, Modri was given a standing ovation and fans held up supportive banners.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> He finished his four-year tenure at Dinamo with a tally of over 31 goals and 29 assists in four league seasons,<sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> contributing most notably in the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_NK_Dinamo_Zagreb_season" title="2007–08 NK Dinamo Zagreb season">2007–08 season</a> when Dinamo won the second <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Croatian_Football_Cup" title="2007–08 Croatian Football Cup">Croatian Cup</a> and became champions by a 28-point margin.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Modri was courted by <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, but opted to wait leaving the club.<sup id="cite_ref-MakingofModric_26-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MakingofModric-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Wilson2016_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wilson2016-47">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Dutch_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dutch-48">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tottenham_Hotspur">Tottenham Hotspur</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Tottenham Hotspur">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2008.E2.80.9310:_Struggle_and_success_in_England"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2008–10:_Struggle_and_success_in_England">2008–10: Struggle and success in England</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2008–10: Struggle and success in England">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kick_Off_(5194424235).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Kick_Off_%285194424235%29.jpg/220px-Kick_Off_%285194424235%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Kick_Off_%285194424235%29.jpg/330px-Kick_Off_%285194424235%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Kick_Off_%285194424235%29.jpg/440px-Kick_Off_%285194424235%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5184" data-file-height="3456" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kick_Off_(5194424235).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri (far left, No. 14), preparing for a match kick-off for <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham</a> against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in November 2010.</div></div></div>
<p>Modri agreed to transfer terms with <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> on 26 April 2008. He was the first of many summer signings for manager <a href="/wiki/Juande_Ramos" title="Juande Ramos">Juande Ramos</a>, and was also the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Premier_League" title="2008–09 Premier League">Premier League</a>'s first summer transfer.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Club chairman <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Levy_(businessman)" title="Daniel Levy (businessman)">Daniel Levy</a> promptly flew to <a href="/wiki/Zagreb" title="Zagreb">Zagreb</a> when <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> and <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> became interested,<sup id="cite_ref-Stand_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stand-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> and after signing a six-year contract, Tottenham confirmed the transfer fee paid was £16.5&#160;million, equalling the club's record fee set by <a href="/wiki/Darren_Bent" title="Darren Bent">Darren Bent</a>'s move in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> He got <a href="/wiki/Squad_number_(association_football)" title="Squad number (association football)">number 14</a> <a href="/wiki/Kit_(association_football)" title="Kit (association football)">jersey</a>, later recalling that he wore it in honour of <a href="/wiki/Johan_Cruyff" title="Johan Cruyff">Johan Cruyff</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-MarcaFFInterview_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcaFFInterview-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Modri made his competitive Premier League debut on 16 August in a 2–1 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Middlesbrough_F.C." title="Middlesbrough F.C.">Middlesbrough</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Riverside_Stadium" title="Riverside Stadium">Riverside Stadium</a> in Spurs' first match of the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._season" title="2008–09 Tottenham Hotspur F.C. season">2008–09 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Modri had a slow start at Tottenham. He suffered from a knee injury early in his tenure and was labelled as a light-weight for the Premier League by sections of the media,<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AlanSmith_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AlanSmith-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> as well as Arsenal manager <a href="/wiki/Ars%C3%A8ne_Wenger" title="Arsène Wenger">Arsène Wenger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Reflecting on that, Modri said that such "critics push you forward to show people they are wrong. Maybe I look lightweight but I am a really strong person mentally and physically, and I never had any problems with my size".<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> This coincided with his poor form, leading to concerns both for himself and Croatia national team head coach <a href="/wiki/Slaven_Bili%C4%87" title="Slaven Bili">Slaven Bili</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Modri spent his early days at a position of number 10, before being shifted to the left wing to play alongside <a href="/wiki/Wilson_Palacios" title="Wilson Palacios">Wilson Palacios</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Spurs teammate <a href="/wiki/Tom_Huddlestone" title="Tom Huddlestone">Tom Huddlestone</a> later said, "[H]is versatility was probably a blessing and a curse, he was that good that he had to play out of position for a bit."<sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the appointment of manager <a href="/wiki/Harry_Redknapp" title="Harry Redknapp">Harry Redknapp</a>, Modri was given a more familiar role as a central or left-sided midfielder, allowing him to have more influence on the team and use his footballing talent more productively, for example in a 4–4 draw with <a href="/wiki/North_London_derby" title="North London derby">arch-rivals</a> Arsenal on 29 October.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Redknapp recognised Modri's value to his side and planned to shape his new team around the Croatian playmaker.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first competitive goal at Tottenham in a 2–2 draw against <a href="/wiki/FC_Spartak_Moscow" title="FC Spartak Moscow">Spartak Moscow</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2008-09_UEFA_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="2008-09 UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a> group stages on 18 December 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first Premier League goals against <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> in an away defeat on 21 December, a home win in the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_FA_Cup" title="2008–09 FA Cup">third round</a> of the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> against <a href="/wiki/Wigan_Athletic_F.C." title="Wigan Athletic F.C.">Wigan Athletic</a> on 2 January 2009, and in an away defeat against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> on 25 April 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Using Modri in his former position from his Dinamo days made him more effective with performances against <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> and most notably on 21 March when he scored the only goal in a win against Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._season" title="2009–10 Tottenham Hotspur F.C. season">2009–10 season</a>, Harry Redknapp said of Modri, "[He's] a hell of a player and a manager's dream, so I am told. He trains like a demon and never complains, will work with and without the ball on the field and can beat a defender with a trick or with a pass. He could get into any team in the top four".<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> On 29 August 2009, during Tottenham's 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Birmingham_City_F.C." title="Birmingham City F.C.">Birmingham City</a>, Modri was taken off injured with a suspected calf injury.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> The following day, it was confirmed Modri had sustained a fracture to his right <a href="/wiki/Fibula" title="Fibula">fibula</a> and was expected to be out for six weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> He returned on 28 December in the <a href="/wiki/London_derbies" title="London derbies">London derby</a> against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>, which Spurs won 2–0 with an 11th-minute goal scored by Modri using the leg he had broken.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> He again scored in a home win against <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> on 28 February 2010,<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> and in an away defeat against <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a> on 9 May.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 30 May 2010, Modri signed a new six-year contract that ran until 2016. Upon signing, he said, "Tottenham Hotspur gave me my chance in the Premier League and I want to go on to achieve great success here with them. Yes, there have been enquiries from other big clubs, but I have no interest in going anywhere. Last season's top-four finish was an indication of where we are as a club and I feel I can continue to improve and go on to achieve everything I want to at Spurs."<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9312:_Outgrowing_Tottenham_Hotspur"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–12:_Outgrowing_Tottenham_Hotspur">2010–12: Outgrowing Tottenham Hotspur</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2010–12: Outgrowing Tottenham Hotspur">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg/140px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="140" height="313" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg/210px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg/280px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="704" data-file-height="1576" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modri%C4%87_2010_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri playing against Arsenal in November 2010.</div></div></div>
<p>On 11 September 2010, Modri scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._season" title="2010–11 Tottenham Hotspur F.C. season">2010–11 season</a> in a 1–1 away draw at <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> On 28 November, in a home match against <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>, Modri scored a goal that was later credited as an <a href="/wiki/Own_goal" title="Own goal">own goal</a> by <a href="/wiki/Martin_%C5%A0krtel" title="Martin Škrtel">Martin Škrtel</a>. After a draw against Manchester United at <a href="/wiki/White_Hart_Lane" title="White Hart Lane">White Hart Lane</a> in January 2011, Redknapp praised Modri, saying, "He was unbelievable. Magnificent. He's an amazing footballer, the little man takes the ball in the tightest areas with people around him, wriggling out of situations. He could play in any team in the world."<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Modri also scored in Tottenham's 3–2 victory over Stoke City on 9 April,<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> and converted a penalty at <a href="/wiki/Anfield" title="Anfield">Anfield</a> on 15 May in a 2–0 victory over Liverpool.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Modri helped Tottenham reach their first involvement in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2010–11 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>. In the first match, against <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> at the <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a> on 20 October, he exited the match early due to injury; Spurs lost 4–3, despite the tremendous efforts of <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Bale" title="Gareth Bale">Gareth Bale</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On the return match at home, on 2 November, Modri was given too much space to move and dictate the tempo of the match. He created and assisted for the first goal by <a href="/wiki/Rafael_van_der_Vaart" title="Rafael van der Vaart">Rafael van der Vaart</a> in a 3–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> In the next match, against <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a>, Modri scored the second goal.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> After a scoreless draw against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Spurs were eliminated from the competition in the quarter-finals by <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Modri played 32 Premier League matches in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Premier_League" title="2010–11 Premier League">2010–11 season</a>, scoring three goals, recording two assists and making the highest average number of passes per match for Spurs with 62.5 and an accuracy rate of 87.4%.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season, Modri was voted the <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C.#Player_of_the_Year" title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur Player of the Year</a>. Then-Manchester United manager <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Sir Alex Ferguson</a> said he would have chosen Modri as his <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">Player of the Year</a> for that season.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:40%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"I spent four great years there with a lot of emotions, with a lot of love from the club and the fans. I enjoyed every moment with Tottenham. But in one moment you feel you need to take a step forward, to go to a higher level. I think it was the right time for me to go, but I will always be thankful to Tottenham for everything they did for me. I became a better player there and they pushed me to this level where I am at the moment."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Luka Modri reflecting on negotiations with Chelsea and move to Real Madrid in February 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>In mid-2011, Modri was heavily pursued by Tottenham's <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C.%E2%80%93Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._rivalry" title="Chelsea F.C.–Tottenham Hotspur F.C. rivalry">London rivals</a> Chelsea, who made a first bid of £22&#160;million, which they increased to £27&#160;million, both of which were rejected by Spurs chairman Daniel Levy.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> After the failed bids, Modri announced he would welcome a move across London and that he had a "gentleman's agreement" with Levy the club would entertain offers from a "big club".<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Speculation continued throughout the summer transfer window, culminating in Modri refusing to play in Tottenham's opening match of the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C._season" title="2011–12 Tottenham Hotspur F.C. season">2011–12 season</a> against Manchester United, which ended in a 3–0 loss.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> Modri said his "head was not in the right place" as he continued to force a move to Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> On the final day of the transfer window, Chelsea made an offer of £40&#160;million that was again rejected.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After failing to secure a transfer, Spurs manager Harry Redknapp told Modri to focus on his playing and named him as a starter.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> On 18 September, he scored his first goal of the season for Tottenham with a shot from 25&#160;yd (23&#160;m) in a 4–0 home win against Liverpool.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> On 14 January 2012, Modri scored the only goal in a home draw with <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolverhampton Wanderers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> On 31 January in a 3–1 win against Wigan Athletic, he assisted for the first goal with a crossfield pass and scored the second from 20&#160;yd (18&#160;m).<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> For the third time that season, he was included in "Team of the Week".<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Modri scored his last goal for Tottenham on 2 May in a 1–4 away win against <a href="/wiki/Bolton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Bolton Wanderers F.C.">Bolton Wanderers</a> with a powerful volley from 25&#160;yd (23&#160;m).<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Real Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313:_Becoming_a_starting_eleven_player_in_Real_Madrid"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012–13:_Becoming_a_starting_eleven_player_in_Real_Madrid">2012–13: Becoming a starting eleven player in Real Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2012–13: Becoming a starting eleven player in Real Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg/170px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="215" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg/255px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg/340px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg 2x" data-file-width="431" data-file-height="545" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modri%C4%87_against_Sevilla.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri playing against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> in February 2013.</div></div></div>
<p>On 27 August 2012, Real Madrid announced they had agreed on a deal with Tottenham for an approximate £30&#160;million transfer fee.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCRM_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCRM-94">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Modri signed a five-year contract with the Spanish club.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCRM_94-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCRM-94">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, he made his Real Madrid debut against Barcelona in the second leg final of the <a href="/wiki/2012_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2012 Supercopa de España">2012 Supercopa de España</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u_Stadium" title="Santiago Bernabéu Stadium">Santiago Bernabéu Stadium</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Mesut_%C3%96zil" title="Mesut Özil">Mesut Özil</a> in the 83rd minute. Madrid won the match, giving Modri his first trophy with the club 36 hours after his signing was announced.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> Despite his positive debut, Modri at first struggled to settle into the team under manager <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> because of his lack of pre-season training, which he missed as a result of his ongoing transfer negotiations.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> The presence of veteran midfielder <a href="/wiki/Xabi_Alonso" title="Xabi Alonso">Xabi Alonso</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sami_Khedira" title="Sami Khedira">Sami Khedira</a> in defensive midfield, and Özil in offensive midfield, usually kept Modri out of the starting line-up, limiting him to substitute appearances. He mostly played out-of-position for his first few months at the club. He played his first <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> match for Real Madrid in the group stage against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> on 18 September, which Madrid won 3–2. On 3 November, Modri scored his first goal for Real Madrid in the last minute of their 4–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Real_Zaragoza" title="Real Zaragoza">Real Zaragoza</a> in <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_La_Liga" title="2012–13 La Liga">La Liga</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> On 17 November, Modri assisted a <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Karim Benzema</a> goal, which was eventually ruled an own goal by <a href="/wiki/Jon_Aurtenetxe" title="Jon Aurtenetxe">Jon Aurtenetxe</a>, with a 50&#160;m (55&#160;yd) cross-field pass. It was the first goal in a 5–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Athletic_Bilbao" title="Athletic Bilbao">Athletic Bilbao</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> His most notable match that year was on 4 December, when he assisted for the first two goals of <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Callej%C3%B3n" title="José Callejón">José Callejón</a> with cross-field passes in a 4–1 victory over Ajax in the group stage of the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the year he was voted as the worst signing of the season by Spanish newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)">Marca</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Modri started in Real Madrid's home match against rivals Barcelona on 2 March 2013. From a corner kick, he assisted <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ramos" title="Sergio Ramos">Sergio Ramos</a> to score the winning goal in the 82nd minute, giving Real a victory in <i><a href="/wiki/El_Cl%C3%A1sico" title="El Clásico">El Clásico</a></i>. On 5 March, Modri came on as a second-half substitute during the decisive Champions League knockout leg against ten-man Manchester United at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a>. With Madrid behind by a goal, Modri equalised with a long-range shot from 25&#160;yd (23&#160;m) out and played a key role in the rest of the match, which Real Madrid won 2–1, advancing them to the quarter-finals 3–2 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> This match is often seen as the turning point in Modri's career in Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> On 16 March, he replicated this performance against <a href="/wiki/RCD_Mallorca" title="RCD Mallorca">Mallorca</a>, giving Real Madrid the lead with a long-range volley from 30&#160;yd (27&#160;m); Real Madrid won the match 5–2.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> Modri played as a starter in both Champions League semi-final matches against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>. In the first leg on 24 April, he played in the attacking midfield position where he did not influence the match and the team lost 4–1. On 30 April, in the second leg 2–0 victory, Modri played as the deep-lying playmaker, making passes to the attackers and creating several chances; he was among the best-rated players that night.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> From March 2013, Modri's form and influence in the midfield continued to improve, distinguishing himself as a player with most passes completed in his team. On 8 May, he assisted from the corner for the first goal and scored the fourth goal in a 6–2 victory over <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A1laga_CF" title="Málaga CF">Málaga</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9315:_Best_midfielder_in_Spain_and_La_D.C3.A9cima"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–15:_Best_midfielder_in_Spain_and_La_Décima">2013–15: Best midfielder in Spain and <i>La Décima</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2013–15: Best midfielder in Spain and La Décima">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:40%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He's the head of midfield in a complicated environment. Every day in Madrid pressure is coming at you from all sides. Modri not only withstands the pressure but has grown among it to be Madrid's best player, with <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">[Cristiano] Ronaldo</a>."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Predrag_Mijatovi%C4%87" title="Predrag Mijatovi">Predrag Mijatovi</a> praises Modri's rising performance and significance for the team in January 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>With the arrival of new manager <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a>, Modri became one of the most frequent starters in the team, being partnered in midfield with Xabi Alonso to provide a balance of defence and attack.<sup id="cite_ref-WhoScored2013_112-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WhoScored2013-112">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> He was consistently the team's most efficient passer, averaging 90% accuracy in <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_La_Liga" title="2013–14 La Liga">La Liga</a>, and also having the most ball recoveries among the squad.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WhoScored2013_112-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WhoScored2013-112">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2013–14 Real Madrid CF season">2013–14 season</a> in the last <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> group match against <a href="/wiki/F.C._Copenhagen" title="F.C. Copenhagen">Copenhagen</a>, making it his fifth goal for the club, all five of which were scored from the outside the penalty area.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> Modri scored his first goal of the Liga season in a 3–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Getafe_CF" title="Getafe CF">Getafe</a>, his sixth goal outside the penalty area.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> Modri was on the pitch when Real Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Copa_del_Rey" title="2013–14 Copa del Rey">2013–14 Copa del Rey</a> after defeating Barcelona 2–1 in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Copa_del_Rey_Final" title="2014 Copa del Rey Final">final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the first leg of the Champions League quarter-finals, Modri intercepted the ball and assisted Cristiano Ronaldo for the third goal in Real Madrid's 3–0 home victory against Borussia Dortmund. The goal was ultimately decisive because Real went on to lose 2–0 in the second leg, but progressed with a marginal aggregate score of 3–2. In his 100th appearance for the club,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Modri assisted for the first goal in the second leg 4–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in the Champions League semi-final, helping Real Madrid reach the final for the first time in 12 years.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> He was included in UEFA's Team of the Week for both legs of the semi-final.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> On 24 May in the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2014 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a>, Modri again assisted from a corner for teammate Sergio Ramos, who scored a 93rd-minute equaliser against <a href="/wiki/Madrid_Derby" title="Madrid Derby">local rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a>. Real won 4–1 in extra time, marking the club's tenth Champions League title, locally known as <i>la Décima</i> ("the tenth").<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> He was included in the UEFA Champions League Team of the Season<sup id="cite_ref-CLTeam20134_122-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CLTeam20134-122">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> and received the <a href="/wiki/LFP_Awards" class="mw-redirect" title="LFP Awards">LFP award</a> for the "Best Midfielder" of the Spanish first league of that season.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August 2014, Modri signed a new contract to stay at Real Madrid until 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> With the departure of Alonso he was partnered with newly arrived <a href="/wiki/Toni_Kroos" title="Toni Kroos">Toni Kroos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> Real Madrid began the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2014–15 Real Madrid CF season">2014–15 season</a> by winning the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2014 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a> over <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> Modri assisted twice for Bale, first against <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a> in <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_La_Liga" title="2014–15 La Liga">La Liga</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> and second against <a href="/wiki/FC_Basel" title="FC Basel">Basel</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> In the 2–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Villarreal_CF" title="Villarreal CF">Villarreal</a>, Modri scored his seventh goal from outside of the box.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In late November, Modri sustained a thigh injury during an international match against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, because of which he did not play for three months.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> He returned in early March 2015, starting in seven matches and proving his form.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> On 21 April, in the 3–1 home win against Málaga, he strained ligaments in his right knee, because of which he did not play until May.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> With his injury, Real Madrid's 22-match winning run in the season came to an end. His absence and the lack of a quality substitute were seen as the main cause of Real Madrid's failure to win matches in La Liga and the Champions League.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Ancelotti said, "Modri has missed most of the year and this has hurt us".<sup id="cite_ref-CollinsTim_137-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CollinsTim-137">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> Modri's influence was recognised and he was selected by professional players in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFPro_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFPro-138">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9317:_Among_best_world_players_and_La_Und.C3.A9cima_and_Duod.C3.A9cima"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–17:_Among_best_world_players_and_La_Undécima_and_Duodécima">2015–17: Among best world players and <i>La Undécima</i> and <i>Duodécima</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2015–17: Among best world players and La Undécima and Duodécima">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Shahter-Reak_M_2015_(10).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2810%29.jpg/170px-Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2810%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="289" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2810%29.jpg/255px-Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2810%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/aa/Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2810%29.jpg/340px-Shahter-Reak_M_2015_%2810%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="493" data-file-height="838" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Shahter-Reak_M_2015_(10).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri playing against <a href="/wiki/FC_Shakhtar_Donetsk" title="FC Shakhtar Donetsk">Shakhtar Donetsk</a> during their <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage#Group_A" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage match</a> in the UEFA Champions League in November 2015.</div></div></div>
<p>For the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2015–16 Real Madrid CF season">2015–16 season</a>, Carlo Ancelotti was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Ben%C3%ADtez" title="Rafael Benítez">Rafael Benítez</a> under whom Modri continued to be a key midfield player.<sup id="cite_ref-Master_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Master-139">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> Modri began the season assisting in September, November and December, and scoring in the 3–4 away win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Shakhtar_Donetsk" title="FC Shakhtar Donetsk">Shakhtar Donetsk</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League group stage">Champions League group stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> He sustained a muscular groin injury during an international match against <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria_national_football_team" title="Bulgaria national football team">Bulgaria</a> in October, initially suggesting an absence of two-to-three weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> However, by 20 October, he had recovered in time for the match against <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>With the arrival of new manager <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> in January 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> the relationship between them was noted in the media, with Modri described as "master of the game",<sup id="cite_ref-Master_139-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Master-139">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> and the crucial "connector" of the defence and attack.<sup id="cite_ref-Connector_146-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Connector-146">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> It was seen in the first three matches, wins against <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo de La Coruña</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sporting_de_Gij%C3%B3n" title="Sporting de Gijón">Sporting de Gijón</a> and a draw against <a href="/wiki/Real_Betis" title="Real Betis">Real Betis</a>, in which Modri was praised for creating chances, his positioning and overall performance and influence.<sup id="cite_ref-Master_139-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Master-139">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Connector_146-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Connector-146">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> On 7 February, Modri scored a winning goal from outside the box in a 1–2 away win against <a href="/wiki/Granada_CF" title="Granada CF">Granada</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> Modri was a regular in the starting line-up when the team won the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16 Champions League</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2016 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a> against Atlético Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> He was included in both Champions League,<sup id="cite_ref-CL_2015/16_Team_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CL_2015/16_Team-150">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> and La Liga's team of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-La_Liga_2015/16_Team_151-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-La_Liga_2015/16_Team-151">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> For the second time, he also received the <a href="/wiki/LFP_Awards" class="mw-redirect" title="LFP Awards">LFP award</a> for the "Best Midfielder" of the Spanish first league.<sup id="cite_ref-LFPAward2_152-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LFPAward2-152">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> He was for the second time included in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFPro2_153-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFPro2-153">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 18 October 2016, Modri signed a new contract with Real Madrid, keeping him at the club until 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> Due to injury of a left knee sustained in mid-September, he missed eight matches, returning early November.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> On 18 December, he won the <a href="/wiki/2016_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2016 FIFA Club World Cup">2016 FIFA Club World Cup</a> with Real Madrid, receiving the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Ball" title="FIFA Club World Cup awards">Silver Ball</a> for his performances during the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-Awards_156-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Awards-156">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> In January 2017, for the first time was included in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> (2016).<sup id="cite_ref-UEFATOTY_157-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFATOTY-157">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> On 12 March 2017, in a 2–1 win over Real Betis, Modri played his 200th match for Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Modri was a regular starter when Real Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">2016–17 La Liga</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> as well as the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">2016–17 UEFA Champions League</a>, where he provided the assist for Cristiano Ronaldo's second goal in the <a href="/wiki/2017_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2017 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> Modri was included in Champions League team of the season<sup id="cite_ref-CL_2016/17_Team_162-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CL_2016/17_Team-162">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> and became the first Croatian to win the Champions League three times.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> He also received the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Football_Awards" title="UEFA Club Football Awards">UEFA Club Football award</a> for Best Midfielder of the Champions League season.<sup id="cite_ref-CLMid2016-2017_164-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CLMid2016-2017-164">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> In the competition for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Men%27s_Player_of_the_Year_Award" title="UEFA Men&#39;s Player of the Year Award">UEFA Men's Player of the Year Award</a>, he came fourth,<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> while for <a href="/wiki/2017_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2017 Ballon d&#39;Or">2017 Ballon d'Or</a>, fifth.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> For the third time, he was also included in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFPro3_167-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFPro3-167">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318:_Ballon_d.27Or_and_third_consecutive_Champions_League_title"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18:_Ballon_d'Or_and_third_consecutive_Champions_League_title">2017–18: Ballon d'Or and third consecutive Champions League title</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2017–18: Ballon d&#039;Or and third consecutive Champions League title">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Liver-RM_(2).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Liver-RM_%282%29.jpg/220px-Liver-RM_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="215" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Liver-RM_%282%29.jpg/330px-Liver-RM_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Liver-RM_%282%29.jpg/440px-Liver-RM_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1022" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Liver-RM_(2).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri (left) with <a href="/wiki/Gareth_Bale" title="Gareth Bale">Gareth Bale</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">2018 Champions League Final</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>With the departure of <a href="/wiki/James_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="James Rodríguez">James Rodríguez</a> to Bayern Munich, Modri inherited the team's coveted <a href="/wiki/Squad_number_(association_football)" title="Squad number (association football)">number 10</a> <a href="/wiki/Kit_(association_football)" title="Kit (association football)">jersey</a> for the new <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2017–18 Real Madrid CF season">2017–18 season</a>, replacing his previous number 19 jersey.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> In December, he won the <a href="/wiki/2017_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2017 FIFA Club World Cup">2017 FIFA Club World Cup</a> with Real Madrid and received the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Ball" title="FIFA Club World Cup awards">Golden Ball</a> award as the best player of the competition for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-MarcaGolden_169-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcaGolden-169">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> His first goal of the season came in a 7–1 win over Deportivo de La Coruña on 21 January 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> In the same month was for the second time included in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> (2017).<sup id="cite_ref-UEFATOTY17_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFATOTY17-171">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> Modri was a regular starter when Real Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 UEFA Champions League</a>, starting in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2018 UEFA Champions League Final">final</a> victory against Liverpool which saw Madrid win their third consecutive title.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> For his performances throughout the campaign, Modri was included in Champions League team of the season for the third consecutive time.<sup id="cite_ref-CL_2017/18_Team_173-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CL_2017/18_Team-173">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> He later received the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Football_Awards#Best_Midfielder" title="UEFA Club Football Awards">UEFA Club Football Award</a> for Best Midfielder of the Champions League season for the second consecutive time.<sup id="cite_ref-CLMid2017-2018_174-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CLMid2017-2018-174">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> In July 2018, it was announced Modri's Real Madrid jersey was
