the most requested jersey of the club after the departure of Cristiano Ronaldo to Juventus.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his club, and national team performance at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, where also received the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Ball" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Golden Ball</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-FIFAGolden_176-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFAGolden-176">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> in August and September Modri won the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Men%27s_Player_of_the_Year_Award" title="UEFA Men&#39;s Player of the Year Award">UEFA Men's Player of the Year Award</a> and <a href="/wiki/The_Best_FIFA_Football_Awards_2018" title="The Best FIFA Football Awards 2018">The Best FIFA Men's Player Award</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-UEFAMPYA_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFAMPYA-177">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIFAPYA_178-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFAPYA-178">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> while in December, he added the <a href="/wiki/2018_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2018 Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a> to his personal tally,<sup id="cite_ref-BBCBallon_179-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCBallon-179">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> marking the first time since <a href="/wiki/2007_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2007 Ballon d&#39;Or">2007</a> that the award was not won by <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> or Cristiano Ronaldo, which polarized the people involved in the sport into two camps about the credibility of the award.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCBallon_179-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCBallon-179">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, besides becoming the first Croatian player to win these awards,<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> Modri was the first player to win both the World Cup Golden Ball and the UEFA Men's Player of the Year Award in the same year since <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> in 1998,<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> and the World Cup Golden Ball and the Best FIFA Men's Player of the Year Award after <a href="/wiki/Rom%C3%A1rio" title="Romário">Romário</a> in 1994.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> Additionally, he is the first player to win the awards from the <a href="/wiki/Former_Yugoslavia" class="mw-redirect" title="Former Yugoslavia">former Yugoslavia</a> territory, the first footballer from <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Europe" title="Eastern Europe">Eastern Europe</a> to win a <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a> after <a href="/wiki/Andriy_Shevchenko" title="Andriy Shevchenko">Andriy Shevchenko</a> in <a href="/wiki/2004_Ballon_d%27Or" title="2004 Ballon d&#39;Or">2004</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> and the tenth player from Real Madrid to capture the trophy.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, winning the trophy triggered a clause in his contract, ensuring his stay at the club until 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> He was also included in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a> for the fourth time,<sup id="cite_ref-FIFPro4_189-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFPro4-189">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup> and won the <a href="/wiki/International_Federation_of_Football_History_%26_Statistics#IFFHS_World&#39;s_Best_Man_Playmaker" title="International Federation of Football History &amp; Statistics">IFFHS World's Best Playmaker</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-IFFHSPlay_190-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IFFHSPlay-190">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After receiving the FIFA Men's Player of the Year Award, Modri stated it "shows that we all can become the best with hard work, dedication, and belief, all dreams can come true".<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> Modri dedicated the Ballon d'Or to "all the players who probably deserved to win it and didn't" in the past decade, including <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Wesley_Sneijder" title="Wesley Sneijder">Wesley Sneijder</a> among others.<sup id="cite_ref-BBCBallon_179-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBCBallon-179">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9321:_Second_time_champion_of_Spain_and_Golden_Foot"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–21:_Second_time_champion_of_Spain_and_Golden_Foot">2018–21: Second time champion of Spain and Golden Foot</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2018–21: Second time champion of Spain and Golden Foot">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The arrival of new manager <a href="/wiki/Julen_Lopetegui" title="Julen Lopetegui">Julen Lopetegui</a> in August 2018 saw Modri given a steady return to the first team as a substitute due to his lack of pre-season training after the 2018 World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> This included a substitute appearance in his team's 2–4 loss after extra time against Atlético Madrid in the <a href="/wiki/2018_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2018 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> His first start of the season came on 1 September in a 4–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/CD_Legan%C3%A9s" title="CD Leganés">Leganés</a>, in which he assisted his side's third goal, scored by Karim Benzema.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> His 100th appearance in the UEFA club competition came on 19 September in a 3–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-ElvirUEFA_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ElvirUEFA-22">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> in which he assisted the second goal, scored by Gareth Bale.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> On 22 December, Modri won his third <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cup</a>, scoring the first goal and assisting for the third in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Al_Ain_FC" title="Al Ain FC">Al Ain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> On 13 and 19 January 2019, Modri for the first time scored in two consecutive league games for Real Madrid, in a 1–2 away win against Real Betis and 2–0 home win against Sevilla.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup> In the same month was included in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> (2018) for the third time in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-UEFATOTY18_200-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UEFATOTY18-200">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> From 27 February to 5 March, Modri went through what he described as "the most difficult week of his football life,"<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup> with Real Madrid losing to Barcelona twice and Ajax and crashing out of <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Copa_del_Rey" title="2018–19 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a>, <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_La_Liga" title="2018–19 La Liga">title</a> race and the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> Despite having had an underwhelming <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2018–19 Real Madrid CF season">season</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Siguero10919_205-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Siguero10919-205">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> for the fifth consecutive time he was included in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFA FIFPro World XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFPro5_206-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFPro5-206">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 August 2019 was the seventh anniversary of Modri's signing with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> Although raising doubts due to age of 34 and decision to continue playing with the national team which makes him prone to injuries,<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup> Modri stated that wants to "recapture his best form this <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2019–20 Real Madrid CF season">season</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-Siguero10919_205-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Siguero10919-205">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> On 1 September and 9 November made his first assists in a 2–2 away draw against Villarreal and in a 0–4 away victory against <a href="/wiki/SD_Eibar" title="SD Eibar">Eibar</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup> while first goal on 5 October in a 4–2 home victory against Granada.<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> On 12 November was awarded with a <a href="/wiki/Golden_Foot" title="Golden Foot">Golden Foot</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-MarcaGoldenFoot_212-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcaGoldenFoot-212">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup> On 23 November he made two assists and scored a goal in a 3–1 home victory against Real Sociedad.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup> On 8 January 2020, Modri scored his fifth goal of the season and 100th career goal in a 3–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> in the semi-finals of <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2019–20 Supercopa de España">2019–20 Supercopa de España</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup> On 12 January he successfully converted a penalty in a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout" title="Penalty shootout">shootout</a> as Real Madrid beat Atlético Madrid 4–1 on penalties in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a_Final" class="mw-redirect" title="2019–20 Supercopa de España Final">final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> Following the continuation of <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="2019–20 La Liga">La Liga</a> after a three month suspension due to <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Spain" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Spain">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, Modri was praised for being one of Real Madrid's best players despite his age, resulting in numerous media outlets wondering about prolongation of his contract with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> On 16 July, he assisted Benzema's opening goal in a 2–1 victory over Villarreal, as Real Madrid secured the league title.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 21 October, he scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Real_Madrid_CF_season" title="2020–21 Real Madrid CF season">2020–21 season</a> in a <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> 3–2 defeat to Shakhtar Donetsk.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup> The goal made him the fourth player in the history of the club to score in the competition aged 35 or more, alongside <a href="/wiki/Alfredo_Di_St%C3%A9fano" title="Alfredo Di Stéfano">Alfredo Di Stéfano</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ferenc_Pusk%C3%A1s" title="Ferenc Puskás">Ferenc Puskás</a> and <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Gento" title="Francisco Gento">Francisco Gento</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup> It was named the Goal of the Week by UEFA.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he came off the bench to score his first ever <i>El Clásico</i> goal, as Real defeated Barcelona 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg/170px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="260" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg/255px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/55/Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg/340px-Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg 2x" data-file-width="784" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modri%C4%87_in_2018.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>. He is said to anchor <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team#Dali_period_and_the_second_&quot;golden_generation&quot;_(2017–present)" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia's second Golden Generation</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Modri began his international career at youth level, playing for the Croatian under-15, <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_under-17_football_team" title="Croatia national under-17 football team">under-17</a>, <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_under-18_football_team" title="Croatia national under-18 football team">under-18</a>, <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_under-19_football_team" title="Croatia national under-19 football team">under-19</a> and <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_under-21_football_team" title="Croatia national under-21 football team">under-21</a> teams.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> He debuted in March 2001 for the under-15 team coached by <a href="/wiki/Martin_Novoselac" title="Martin Novoselac">Martin Novoselac</a>, but nevertheless his talent and psychological maturity, he did not become a regular starter and leading player until physically strengthened and debuted for under-18. Novoselac considers him as a model for all young players because is a result of a gradual and continuous work and effort, as well as talent.<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201644–45_224-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEAzpitartePuertas201644–45-224">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> Modri made his full international debut for <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a> on 1 March 2006 in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> in <a href="/wiki/Basel" title="Basel">Basel</a>, which Croatia won 3–2.<sup id="cite_ref-Mid_38-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mid-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2006.E2.80.9308:_2006_World_Cup_and_Euro_2008"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2006–08:_2006_World_Cup_and_Euro_2008">2006–08: 2006 World Cup and Euro 2008</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 2006–08: 2006 World Cup and Euro 2008">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Modri made two appearances at the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 FIFA World Cup</a> finals as a substitute in the group fixtures against <a href="/wiki/Japan_national_football_team" title="Japan national football team">Japan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_soccer_team" title="Australia national soccer team">Australia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> With the appointment of new manager Slaven Bili, Modri earned greater recognition at international level; he scored his first goal in Croatia's 2–0 friendly win over <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2006 FIFA World Cup Final">world champions</a> Italy on 16 August 2006 in <a href="/wiki/Livorno" title="Livorno">Livorno</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Modri's performances ensured a regular place in the international side and he gave a successful showing in Croatia's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_qualifying_Group_E" title="UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying Group E">UEFA Euro 2008 qualifying campaign</a>, which included home and away victories against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> As a young midfielder, much was expected of Modri; he was often dubbed "the Croatian Cruyff".<sup id="cite_ref-Dutch_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dutch-48">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup> Modri scored Croatia's first goal of <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">Euro 2008</a>, converting a penalty in the fourth minute of their 1–0 victory against hosts <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a> on 8 June 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup> It was the fastest penalty ever awarded and scored in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">European Championship</a> history.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup> He continued to impress at the tournament and was named <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_Match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the Match">Man of the Match</a> in Croatia's next match when they defeated one of the pre-tournament favourites and eventual <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2008 Final">finalists</a> <a href="/wiki/German_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="German national football team">Germany</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-modricman_233-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-modricman-233">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> In the quarter-final against <a href="/wiki/Turkey_national_football_team" title="Turkey national football team">Turkey</a>, Modri took advantage of a mistake by veteran Turkish goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/R%C3%BC%C5%9Ft%C3%BC_Re%C3%A7ber" title="Rütü Reçber">Rütü Reçber</a>, and crossed to teammate <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Klasni%C4%87" title="Ivan Klasni">Ivan Klasni</a> for the first goal of the match with one minute of extra time remaining, but <a href="/wiki/Semih_%C5%9Eent%C3%BCrk" title="Semih entürk">Semih entürk</a> almost immediately equalised for Turkey. In the ensuing penalty shootout, Modri's kick was off-target and he failed to score the first penalty and Turkey won the shootout 3–1.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the competition, Modri was included in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008#UEFA_Team_of_the_Tournament" title="UEFA Euro 2008">UEFA Team of the Tournament</a>, becoming only the second Croatian to achieve this honour after <a href="/wiki/Davor_%C5%A0uker" title="Davor Šuker">Davor Šuker</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Dalje_2008_235-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dalje_2008-235">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2008.E2.80.9316:_Subsequent_struggles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2008–16:_Subsequent_struggles">2008–16: Subsequent struggles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 2008–16: Subsequent struggles">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_6" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Group 6">2010 World Cup qualifiers</a>, Modri scored three goals, against <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan_national_football_team" title="Kazakhstan national football team">Kazakhstan</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_football_team" title="Andorra national football team">Andorra</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> matching <a href="/wiki/Ivica_Oli%C4%87" title="Ivica Oli">Ivica Oli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Rakiti%C4%87" title="Ivan Rakiti">Ivan Rakiti</a> and Eduardo. The team failed to qualify finishing one point behind second-placed Ukraine. After appearing in all of their <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_Group_F" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying Group F">UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying</a> matches and scoring a goal against <a href="/wiki/Israel_national_football_team" title="Israel national football team">Israel</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup> Modri started in all three of Croatia <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Group_C" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Group C">group stage</a> matches against the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a>, Italy and <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>, but the team failed to progress. His most notable performance was against Spain. The most memorable moment of the match came when Modri picked the ball on the halfway line skipping Spain's midfield trio, rushing down on the right to reach the penalty area where he evaded a defender and crossed from 18&#160;yd (16&#160;m) to Ivan Rakiti, but <a href="/wiki/Iker_Casillas" title="Iker Casillas">Iker Casillas</a> saved this attempt.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup> Because Croatia did not advance from the group stage, Modri was not included in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012#Awards" title="UEFA Euro 2012">Team of the Tournament</a>, although <i><a href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" title="The Daily Telegraph">The Daily Telegraph</a></i> included him in the best 11 until the semi-finals,<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup> and his play was well received by critics.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_(10).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_%2810%29.jpg/220px-Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_%2810%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="137" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_%2810%29.jpg/330px-Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_%2810%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_%2810%29.jpg/440px-Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_%2810%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4928" data-file-height="3058" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Brazil_and_Croatia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-06-12_(10).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri playing against <a href="/wiki/Neymar" title="Neymar">Neymar</a> of <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Second_Round" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Second Round">playoffs</a>, Modri with the Croatian team qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>. They entered <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_Group_A" title="2014 FIFA World Cup Group A">Group A</a> with hosts <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cameroon_national_football_team" title="Cameroon national football team">Cameroon</a>. Croatia played the opening match against Brazil, which they lost 3–1,<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup> and Modri sustained a minor foot injury.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup> In the second match, Croatia won 4–0 against Cameroon,<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup> but did not progress to the knockout stage after losing 3–1 to Mexico,<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup> despite the great expectations from the Croatian press and public.<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_qualifying_Group_H" title="UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying Group H">Euro 2016 qualifying</a> rounds, Modri scored his first goals for Croatia in three years, the first against <a href="/wiki/Malta_national_football_team" title="Malta national football team">Malta</a> on his 29th birthday with a long-range shot,<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">&#91;249&#93;</a></sup> then a penalty against <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan_national_football_team" title="Azerbaijan national football team">Azerbaijan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">&#91;250&#93;</a></sup> On 3 March 2015, Modri captained Croatia for the first time, in an away draw against Azerbaijan.<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">&#91;251&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">tournament</a> proper, Modri scored the match-winning goal in Croatia's opening <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_Group_D" title="UEFA Euro 2016 Group D">group stage</a> match against Turkey, a <a href="/wiki/Volley_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Volley (football)">volley</a> from 25 metres (28 yards).<sup id="cite_ref-Match_vs_Turkey_254-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Match_vs_Turkey-254">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup> In so doing, he became the first Croatian to score at the finals of two separate European Championships, having previously scored against Austria in 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">&#91;253&#93;</a></sup> He was named Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-Match_vs_Turkey_254-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Match_vs_Turkey-254">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup> Modri was forced to miss the crucial fixture against Spain on 21 June because of a minor muscle injury.<sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup> However, Croatia won and topped the group,<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;256&#93;</a></sup> but lost to <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> 0–1 in extra-time in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_knockout_phase#Croatia_vs_Portugal" title="UEFA Euro 2016 knockout phase">round of 16</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;257&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2016.E2.80.9318:_Golden_Ball_of_the_2018_World_Cup"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–18:_Golden_Ball_of_the_2018_World_Cup">2016–18: Golden Ball of the 2018 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 2016–18: Golden Ball of the 2018 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg/170px-Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="215" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg/255px-Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg/340px-Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg 2x" data-file-width="781" data-file-height="990" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Modri%C4%87_World_Cup_2018.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Modri with Croatia during the World Cup.</div></div></div>
<p>For Croatia's <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_I" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Group I">2018 World Cup qualifying campaign</a>, Modri became the new team captain, following <a href="/wiki/Darijo_Srna" title="Darijo Srna">Darijo Srna</a>'s retirement.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup> Croatia started the campaign well; however, following 1–0 defeats to <a href="/wiki/Iceland_national_football_team" title="Iceland national football team">Iceland</a><sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup> and Turkey<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup> and a 1–1 draw with <a href="/wiki/Finland_national_football_team" title="Finland national football team">Finland</a> (in which Modri made his <a href="/wiki/List_of_men%27s_footballers_with_100_or_more_international_caps" title="List of men&#39;s footballers with 100 or more international caps">100th appearance for the national team</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">&#91;261&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">&#91;262&#93;</a></sup> Croatia seriously compromised their qualification for the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">&#91;263&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">&#91;264&#93;</a></sup> This caused Modri to publicly state his lack of confidence in coach <a href="/wiki/Ante_%C4%8Ca%C4%8Di%C4%87" title="Ante ai">Ante ai</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">&#91;265&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">&#91;266&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">&#91;267&#93;</a></sup> ai was soon replaced by <a href="/wiki/Zlatko_Dali%C4%87" title="Zlatko Dali">Zlatko Dali</a> ahead of Croatia's final qualifier against Ukraine away,<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">&#91;268&#93;</a></sup> which Croatia won 2–0 and won a place in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Second_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Second Round">play-offs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">&#91;269&#93;</a></sup> Modri scored a penalty in the 4–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Greece_national_football_team" title="Greece national football team">Greece</a> in the second qualifying round,<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;270&#93;</a></sup> enabling his team to qualify for the World Cup.
</p><p>Croatia were placed in <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Group_D" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Group D">Group D</a> alongside Argentina, Iceland and <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a>. During the tournament, Modri—along with Ivan Rakiti and Mario Mandžuki—were referred to as <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team#Dali_period_and_the_second_&quot;golden_generation&quot;_(2017–present)" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia's second "Golden Generation"</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;271&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup> In Croatia's opening win against Nigeria, Modri once again successfully executed a penalty kick and was named Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">&#91;273&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276">&#91;274&#93;</a></sup> He also scored in Croatia's subsequent 3–0 win over Argentina with a long-range shot from 25 yards (23 metres),<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">&#91;275&#93;</a></sup> also being named Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278">&#91;276&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279">&#91;277&#93;</a></sup> After also featuring in the final group stage match, against Iceland, his performances in the first round of the tournament saw him ranked by <i><a href="/wiki/FourFourTwo" title="FourFourTwo">FourFourTwo</a></i>, <i>The Daily Telegraph</i> and <a href="/wiki/ESPN" title="ESPN">ESPN</a> as the best player of the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-280" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-280">&#91;278&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281">&#91;279&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282">&#91;280&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Croatia_vs_Denmark" title="2018 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">round of 16</a> against <a href="/wiki/Denmark_national_football_team" title="Denmark national football team">Denmark</a> on 1 July, with the score tied at 1–1, Modri created a goalscoring opportunity for <a href="/wiki/Ante_Rebi%C4%87" title="Ante Rebi">Ante Rebi</a> in the second half of extra-time, who was brought down in the penalty area; Modri proceeded to take the penalty, but his strike was saved by <a href="/wiki/Kasper_Schmeichel" title="Kasper Schmeichel">Kasper Schmeichel</a>. However, Modri managed to score his spot-kick during the ensuing penalty shoot-out and Croatia advanced to the next round following a 3–2 victory on penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-283" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-283">&#91;281&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284">&#91;282&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285">&#91;283&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Russia_vs_Croatia" title="2018 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">quarter-finals</a> against hosts <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a> on 7 July, Modri provided an assist in extra-time for <a href="/wiki/Domagoj_Vida" title="Domagoj Vida">Domagoj Vida</a> from a corner kick, and once again scored in the victorious penalty shoot-out following a 2–2 draw; he was named Man of the Match for the third time in the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">&#91;284&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">&#91;285&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-final against England on 11 July, Croatia advanced to the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">World Cup final</a> for the first time in their history following a 2–1 victory in extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288">&#91;286&#93;</a></sup> It was reported two days before the final match that Modri ran the most miles out of any player and was third by created chances, as well had most dribbles per match and completed passes in the opponent's half in his team.<sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289">&#91;287&#93;</a></sup> Although Croatia were beaten 4–2 by <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> in the final on 15 July,<sup id="cite_ref-McNulty_290-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McNulty-290">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup> Modri was awarded the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Golden_Ball" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Golden Ball</a> for the best player of the tournament,<sup id="cite_ref-FIFAGolden_176-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFAGolden-176">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> and was included in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup#Dream_Team" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">Team of the Tournament</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FIFATEAM1_291-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFATEAM1-291">&#91;289&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FIFATEAM2_292-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FIFATEAM2-292">&#91;290&#93;</a></sup> After the squad's huge welcome in Zagreb,<sup id="cite_ref-293" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-293">&#91;291&#93;</a></sup> Modri and his teammates <a href="/wiki/Danijel_Suba%C5%A1i%C4%87" title="Danijel Subaši">Danijel Subaši</a>, <a href="/wiki/%C5%A0ime_Vrsaljko" title="Šime Vrsaljko">Šime Vrsaljko</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dominik_Livakovi%C4%87" title="Dominik Livakovi">Dominik Livakovi</a> were welcomed by tens of thousands of people in their hometown of Zadar.<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294">&#91;292&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2018.E2.80.9320:_Post-World_Cup_period"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–20:_Post-World_Cup_period">2018–20: Post-World Cup period</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 2018–20: Post-World Cup period">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Modri took part in all four matches in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Nations League">inaugural edition</a> of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a> as Croatia finished at the bottom of <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Nations_League_A#Group_4" title="2018–19 UEFA Nations League A">Group A4</a> following historical 6–0 away defeat to Spain in September and a 2–1 defeat to England at the <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a> in November.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020_qualifying_Group_E" title="UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying Group E">Euro 2020 qualifying</a> rounds, Modri scored two goals; a penalty in the away 1–1 draw with Azerbaijan and a solo-effort in the home 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungary</a> as Croatia topped the group and qualified for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020" title="UEFA Euro 2020">tournament</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-295" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-295">&#91;293&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">&#91;294&#93;</a></sup> However, due to the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Europe" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Europe">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, the tournament was postponed for a year.<sup id="cite_ref-297" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-297">&#91;295&#93;</a></sup> In September 2020, ahead of Croatia's <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Nations_League_A#Group_3" title="2020–21 UEFA Nations League A">Nations League</a> away fixtures against Portugal and France, head coach Dali allowed Modri to withdraw from the squad in order to prepare well for the upcoming club season.<sup id="cite_ref-298" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-298">&#91;296&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Player_profile">Player profile</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Player profile">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:20%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Not only is he a very hard worker, he has a good brain and he provided some calmness and composure to the <a href="/wiki/Midfield" title="Midfield">midfield</a>. His passing was neat and his contribution was outstanding. He was not only winning the ball, he was passing well. We thought that he was very influential. He did not just work hard, he made the other people play well around him".</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">–<a href="/wiki/G%C3%A9rard_Houllier" title="Gérard Houllier">Gérard Houllier</a>, UEFA Technical Team<sup id="cite_ref-modricman_233-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-modricman-233">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>A diminutive midfielder, Modri is described as a quick and creative <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a>, with great vision, who is able to change the course of the game with incredibly deft passes and solo, long-range efforts.<sup id="cite_ref-ESPN_299-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ESPN-299">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup> He plays with both feet in combination with his swift offensive positioning, off the ball.<sup id="cite_ref-modricability_300-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-modricability-300">&#91;298&#93;</a></sup> He passes the ball accurately across long and short distances (passing range of perfection), even with the outside of his boot. His ball control, first touch, positional play,<sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup> ability to retain possession,<sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> and set the tempo of the game makes him a mesmerising player to watch.<sup id="cite_ref-TheHail2017_302-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheHail2017-302">&#91;300&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303">&#91;301&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-304" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-304">&#91;302&#93;</a></sup> A former <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-I_can_play_anywhere_in_midfield_305-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-I_can_play_anywhere_in_midfield-305">&#91;303&#93;</a></sup> he is also noted for his <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills<sup id="cite_ref-306" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-306">&#91;304&#93;</a></sup> and is considered a master of the "pre-<a href="/wiki/Assist_(association_football)" title="Assist (association football)">assist</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He has also been known to take <a href="/wiki/Free_kick_(association_football)" title="Free kick (association football)">set pieces</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-307" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-307">&#91;305&#93;</a></sup> He is referred to as the Midfield <i><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/maestro" class="extiw" title="wikt:maestro">Maestro</a></i> ("Midfield Master")<sup id="cite_ref-308" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-308">&#91;306&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-309" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-309">&#91;307&#93;</a></sup> for his mastery of footballing fundamentals, tactical strategy, and precision in execution.<sup id="cite_ref-TheHail2017_302-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TheHail2017-302">&#91;300&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310">&#91;308&#93;</a></sup> His tactical vision and strategic planning has had him compared to a <a href="/wiki/Conducting" title="Conducting">conductor of an orchestra</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CollinsTim_137-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CollinsTim-137">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-311" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-311">&#91;309&#93;</a></sup> a "<a href="/wiki/Puppeteer" title="Puppeteer">Puppet Master</a>",<sup id="cite_ref-312" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-312">&#91;310&#93;</a></sup> and a "Midfield Magician".<sup id="cite_ref-313" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-313">&#91;311&#93;</a></sup> After moving to Real Madrid, he was nicknamed by the Spanish media as <i>El <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/p%C3%A1jaro" class="extiw" title="wikt:pájaro">Pájaro</a></i> ("the bird").<sup id="cite_ref-314" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-314">&#91;312&#93;</a></sup> In the dressing room, he is affectionately called "Lukita".<sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315">&#91;313&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Position">Position</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Position">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Modri's complex game has brought him consistent success in the clubs for which he has played. Initially a <a href="/wiki/Playmaker#Advanced_playmakers" title="Playmaker">trequartista</a> or attacking midfielder at Dinamo Zagreb and in his early career at Tottenham, in the 2010–11 season he flourished in a central midfield role as a deep-lying playmaker (regista) who conducts the attack and creates chances for teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-WhoscoredAsset11_316-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WhoscoredAsset11-316">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, Modri acknowledged the role that <a href="/wiki/Harry_Redknapp" title="Harry Redknapp">Harry Redknapp</a> played in shaping of deep-lying his style, saying that dropping back enabled him "to read the game better" and show his full "creativity".<sup id="cite_ref-317" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-317">&#91;315&#93;</a></sup> Although a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, Modri is also a hard-working player who has been seen to adopt a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfield</a> role in addition to playmaking, tracking back to win the ball from the opposition and prepare for a counter-attack, making him one of the most versatile players in the world, capable of playing in several <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfield</a> positions.<sup id="cite_ref-modricability_300-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-modricability-300">&#91;298&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-I_can_play_anywhere_in_midfield_305-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-I_can_play_anywhere_in_midfield-305">&#91;303&#93;</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Wilson_(writer)" title="Jonathan Wilson (writer)">Jonathan Wilson</a>, in a 4–2–3–1 system Modri is a third type of a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">holding midfielder</a>, being "neither entirely destructive or creative", but a "carrier" who is "capable of making late runs or carrying the ball at his feet", but in his case "with a hint of <i>regista</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318">&#91;316&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The switch to a more deep-lying position reduced his number of assists and goals, as well as his shot per game count (1.2), although his game was no longer based on being a goal threat; despite this, he had the second-highest count of key passes per game (2.06) in the team, as well as a very high pass accuracy rate (87%), with the highest passes per game count (62.5) in the team, the most long balls per game (5.6), the most successful dribbles (2.2), interceptions (2.5), and the highest tackle (1.9) count per game among others, high statistics which placed him amongst the top midfielders of the Premier League.<sup id="cite_ref-WhoscoredAsset11_316-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WhoscoredAsset11-316">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319">&#91;317&#93;</a></sup> By the 2011–12 season statistically he was among the top-rated central and all-round midfielders across the top five leagues, alongside players like <a href="/wiki/Xabi_Alonso" title="Xabi Alonso">Xabi Alonso</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Pirlo" title="Andrea Pirlo">Andrea Pirlo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bastian_Schweinsteiger" title="Bastian Schweinsteiger">Bastian Schweinsteiger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320">&#91;318&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321">&#91;319&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon Modri's arrival to Real Madrid, his midfield position was described as <a href="/wiki/Squad_number_(association_football)" title="Squad number (association football)">numbers</a> six (defensive), eight (central) or ten (attacking), depending on the tactics,<sup id="cite_ref-Mourinho_on_LM_322-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mourinho_on_LM-322">&#91;320&#93;</a></sup> and his role was described as the second <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deep-lying pivot</a> alongside Xabi Alonso in the 2012–13 season, a classic deep-lying playmaker whose creativity was needed to dictate his team's play and unlock the opposing defence.<sup id="cite_ref-SN_Plan_C_323-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SN_Plan_C-323">&#91;321&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-324" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-324">&#91;322&#93;</a></sup> In the first half of the 2013–14 season, during which he formed an effective central midfield partnership with Alonso and <a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Di_Mar%C3%ADa" title="Ángel Di María">Ángel Di María</a>, Modri made more tackles (56) than any other Real Madrid player in La Liga with an average number of 2.86 tackles per match, as well as making the most completed passes (878) in the opposition half of the pitch among Real Madrid players, with the highest passing accuracy in La Liga (90%) (also the highest of any midfielder in Europe's top five leagues who have made five or more assists during the season).<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> In the 2014–15 season, with the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Toni_Kroos" title="Toni Kroos">Toni Kroos</a>, Real Madrid no longer had an effective and natural ball-winner alongside their playmakers in midfield, while the team possessed many attackers. Therefore, in addition to producing the highest count of passes (60.7–64.7) and key passes per match (0.8–1.2) within the team, both Modri and Kroos had more defensive responsibility to set the rhythm of the team's gameplay in midfield and orchestrate counterattacks.<sup id="cite_ref-Tweedale2014_325-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tweedale2014-325">&#91;323&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-326" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-326">&#91;324&#93;</a></sup> Modri's average passing accuracy during the season was between 91.6–92%, while his highest completion rate in a single match occurred in October against Barcelona when he completed all 42 attempted passes.<sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327">&#91;325&#93;</a></sup> For all of 2014, Modri's dribble attempts (75) at a success rate of 76% were second in Europe's top five leagues.<sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328">&#91;326&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Reception">Reception</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Reception">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal,_10th_June_2013_(2).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal%2C_10th_June_2013_%282%29.jpg/220px-Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal%2C_10th_June_2013_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal%2C_10th_June_2013_%282%29.jpg/330px-Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal%2C_10th_June_2013_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal%2C_10th_June_2013_%282%29.jpg/440px-Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal%2C_10th_June_2013_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4555" data-file-height="3036" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Luka_Modric_-_Croatia_vs._Portugal,_10th_June_2013_(2).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Considered the most versatile and critical member of the national team, Modri's technical ability has been heralded by both players and coaches.</div></div></div>
<p>Modri is widely regarded as one of most well-rounded and effective midfielders in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-Tweedale2014_325-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tweedale2014-325">&#91;323&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ReviewDiario2016_329-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReviewDiario2016-329">&#91;327&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-RankedESPN2016_330-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RankedESPN2016-330">&#91;328&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BestWorldSoccer2017_331-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BestWorldSoccer2017-331">&#91;329&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SBTB2017_332-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SBTB2017-332">&#91;330&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ShadowsMarca2017_333-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ShadowsMarca2017-333">&#91;331&#93;</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Wilson_(writer)" title="Jonathan Wilson (writer)">Jonathan Wilson</a>, what sets apart Modri from old-school playmakers (number ten) like <a href="/wiki/Juan_Rom%C3%A1n_Riquelme" title="Juan Román Riquelme">Juan Román Riquelme</a> is the universality due to increased defensive responsibility, a quality which was insisted by <a href="/wiki/Valeriy_Lobanovskyi" title="Valeriy Lobanovskyi">Valeriy Lobanovskyi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arrigo_Sacchi" title="Arrigo Sacchi">Arrigo Sacchi</a> that should make a modern footballer.<sup id="cite_ref-334" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-334">&#91;332&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-335" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-335">&#91;333&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Modri's skill in the game was recognised early by <a href="/wiki/Dragan_Stojkovi%C4%87" title="Dragan Stojkovi">Dragan "Piksi" Stojkovi</a>, who stated, "I saw a small blond boy who played exactly like I would. Ideas he was showing then on the terrain were fascinating".<sup id="cite_ref-Piksi_336-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Piksi-336">&#91;334&#93;</a></sup> Piksi considered him, along with <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9s_Iniesta" title="Andrés Iniesta">Andrés Iniesta</a>, as the most intelligent player.<sup id="cite_ref-Piksi_336-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Piksi-336">&#91;334&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Johan_Cruyff" title="Johan Cruyff">Johan Cruyff</a> said Modri's quality and influence on the game depend on the freedom he gets.<sup id="cite_ref-337" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-337">&#91;335&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Paul_Scholes" title="Paul Scholes">Paul Scholes</a>, who played several times against Modri, said in an interview with the <i><a href="/wiki/Manchester_Evening_News" title="Manchester Evening News">Manchester Evening News</a></i> in 2011, "Of the three (<a href="/wiki/Samir_Nasri" title="Samir Nasri">Samir Nasri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wesley_Sneijder" title="Wesley Sneijder">Wesley Sneijder</a>), Modri, has been the one I have been most impressed with, [and] whenever we played Tottenham, he was the one who stood out".<sup id="cite_ref-338" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-338">&#91;336&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, Zinedine Zidane included Modri in his best XI currently playing the game,<sup id="cite_ref-339" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-339">&#91;337&#93;</a></sup> while in January 2016 in private meeting with Modri he told him that he saw him as a player who could win Ballon d'Or.<sup id="cite_ref-MarcaFFInterview_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MarcaFFInterview-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, <a href="/wiki/Gennaro_Gattuso" title="Gennaro Gattuso">Gennaro Gattuso</a> stated that he would have loved to have played with Modri, calling him "an incredible player, really strong mentally and a pure footballer".<sup id="cite_ref-340" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-340">&#91;338&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, <a href="/wiki/Andriy_Shevchenko" title="Andriy Shevchenko">Andriy Shevchenko</a> has stated that he considers Modri to be one of the greatest midfielders to ever play.<sup id="cite_ref-341" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-341">&#91;339&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, <a href="/wiki/Robert_Prosine%C4%8Dki" title="Robert Prosineki">Robert Prosineki</a>, with whom <a href="/wiki/Ivan_Rakiti%C4%87" title="Ivan Rakiti">Ivan Rakiti</a> agreed, considered Modri as the best Croatian player in the history.<sup id="cite_ref-Stand_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stand-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-342" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-342">&#91;340&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-343" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-343">&#91;341&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Davor_%C5%A0uker" title="Davor Šuker">Davor Šuker</a> also considered him as the greatest Croatian footballer of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-344" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-344">&#91;342&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Predrag_Mijatovi%C4%87" title="Predrag Mijatovi">Predrag Mijatovi</a> considered him as the best footballer in the history of the region of <a href="/wiki/Balkans" title="Balkans">Balkans</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-345" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-345">&#91;343&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> said he wanted Modri in Real Madrid because of his influence on the game, tactical level and because he has "that artistic sense".<sup id="cite_ref-Mourinho_on_LM_322-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mourinho_on_LM-322">&#91;320&#93;</a></sup> In 2012, <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a> praised Modri's technique and versatility as a midfield player, stating, "Modri is an outstanding player and in my opinion one of the best midfielders in the world right now, because he can play in more than one position".<sup id="cite_ref-346" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-346">&#91;344&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-347" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-347">&#91;345&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Alex Ferguson</a> regarded him highly as a player while he played in the Premier League, saying it is fair to compare him to Paul Scholes because both are intelligent footballers with good passing consistencies, control of the game, fairplay,<sup id="cite_ref-348" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-348">&#91;346&#93;</a></sup> and wanted to sign him.<sup id="cite_ref-Stand_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stand-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-349" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-349">&#91;347&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Slaven_Bili%C4%87" title="Slaven Bili">Slaven Bili</a> said Modri "is a player who makes others better, they all benefit from him being in the team. He's not selfish, he's playing for the team&#160;...&#160;he's a complete player; good in defence, good in offence—it looks like he was born with the ball at his feet".<sup id="cite_ref-Ice_Cold_55-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ice_Cold-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Others managers who have praised Modri's game include <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-350" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-350">&#91;348&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Sven-G%C3%B6ran_Eriksson" title="Sven-Göran Eriksson">Sven-Göran Eriksson</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-351" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-351">&#91;349&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Modri married Vanja Bosni in May 2010 in the Croatian capital <a href="/wiki/Zagreb" title="Zagreb">Zagreb</a> in a private ceremony after four years of dating,<sup id="cite_ref-352" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-352">&#91;350&#93;</a></sup> and a year later in church.<sup id="cite_ref-353" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-353">&#91;351&#93;</a></sup> Their son, Ivano, was born on 6 June 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-Football_star_Luka_Modric_becomes_a_father_354-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Football_star_Luka_Modric_becomes_a_father-354">&#91;352&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Modric_family_idyll_355-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Modric_family_idyll-355">&#91;353&#93;</a></sup> Their daughter, Ema, was born on 25 April 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-Modric_family_idyll_355-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Modric_family_idyll-355">&#91;353&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-356" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-356">&#91;354&#93;</a></sup> Their second daughter, Sofia, was born on 2 October 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-357" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-357">&#91;355&#93;</a></sup> Modri generally maintains a low profile outside of football.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Interview2014_37-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Interview2014-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-358" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-358">&#91;356&#93;</a></sup> In addition to his native <a href="/wiki/Croatian_language" title="Croatian language">Croatian</a>, Modri also speaks <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-359" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-359">&#91;357&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-360" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-360">&#91;358&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-361" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-361">&#91;359&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-362" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-362">&#91;360&#93;</a></sup> and is <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church_in_Croatia" title="Catholic Church in Croatia">Roman Catholic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-363" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-363">&#91;361&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-364" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-364">&#91;362&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In late 2019, Modri released his autobiography <i>Moja igra</i> (<i>My Game</i>), co-written by prominent Croatian sports journalist Robert Matteoni.<sup id="cite_ref-365" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-365">&#91;363&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-366" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-366">&#91;364&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legal_issues">Legal issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Legal issues">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In March 2018, in an <a href="/wiki/Embezzlement" title="Embezzlement">embezzlement</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tax_evasion" title="Tax evasion">tax evasion</a> trial against the former Dinamo Zagreb executive, <a href="/wiki/Zdravko_Mami%C4%87" title="Zdravko Mami">Zdravko Mami</a>, Modri was called as a witness.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_367-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-367">&#91;365&#93;</a></sup> Throughout the mid-late 2000s, Modri signed multiple contracts with Mami to play at Dinamo Zagreb.<sup id="cite_ref-368" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-368">&#91;366&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-SkyBate_369-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SkyBate-369">&#91;367&#93;</a></sup> Modri <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/annex" class="extiw" title="wiktionary:annex">annexed</a> most of his Tottenham transfer fee to Mami because he was the broker of the move and gave Modri financial backing early on in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-370" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-370">&#91;368&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-371" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-371">&#91;369&#93;</a></sup> Despite stating in 2017 that he signed the annexe clause of the contract ten years earlier, in his testimony he stated that he signed it in 2004, the year of his first contract. Modri was <a href="/wiki/Criminal_charge" title="Criminal charge">charged</a> with <a href="/wiki/Perjury" title="Perjury">perjury</a> for stating that he annexed his fee at an earlier date than he allegedly had.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_367-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-367">&#91;365&#93;</a></sup> Facing the judge, he said, "I came here to state my defence and tell the truth, like every time so far. My conscience is clear".<sup id="cite_ref-SkyBate_369-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SkyBate-369">&#91;367&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-372" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-372">&#91;370&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Croatian_Football_Federation" title="Croatian Football Federation">Croatian Football Federation</a> stood behind Modri,<sup id="cite_ref-SkyBate_369-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-SkyBate-369">&#91;367&#93;</a></sup> but a part of the Croatian public, frustrated with the corruption in Croatian football, perceived the alleged perjury as a defence of Mami and became critical of Modri.<sup id="cite_ref-373" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-373">&#91;371&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-374" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-374">&#91;372&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-375" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-375">&#91;373&#93;</a></sup> Some international news outlets praised him for dealing with the stress of his legal situation while performing with the Croatian team at the 2018 FIFA World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-376" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-376">&#91;374&#93;</a></sup> In October and December 2018, the perjury charge was rejected by the Croatian courts.<sup id="cite_ref-377" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-377">&#91;375&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-378" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-378">&#91;376&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Luka_Modri%C4%87&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

"<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.index.hr/sport/clanak/ekskluzivno-pedja-mijatovic-naklonio-se-hrvatskoj-i-modricu-luka-je-najbolji-igrac-u-povijesti-balkana/2010301.aspx">Exclusive: Pea Mijatovi bowed to Croatia and Modri: "Luka is the best footballer in the history of Balkans"</a>" (in Croatian). <a href="/wiki/Index.hr" title="Index.hr">Index.hr</a>. Retrieved 22 November 2018.</li>

</span></li>

<li id="cite_note-17"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-17">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r999302996"/><cite id="CITEREFRadoš2013" class="citation web cs1">Radoš, Ivica (9 March 2013). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.vecernji.hr/premium/luka-modric-odrastanje-i-karijera-521273">"Luka Modri, odrastanje i karijera"</a> &#91;Luka Modri, rising up and career&#93;. <i>Veernji list</i> (in Croatian)<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">23 June</span> 2018</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=Ve%C4%8Dernji+list&amp;rft.atitle=Luka+Modri%C4%87%2C+odrastanje+i+karijera&amp;rft.date=2013-03-09&amp;rft.aulast=Rado%C5%A1&amp;rft.aufirst=Ivica&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.vecernji.hr%2Fpremium%2Fluka-modric-odrastanje-i-karijera-521273&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALuka+Modri%C4%87" class="Z3988"></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-FOOTNOTEop201416-18"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-FOOTNOTEop201416_18-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFop2014">op 2014</a>, p.&#160;16.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-FOOTNOTEModriMatteoni20205–6-19"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-FOOTNOTEModriMatteoni20205–6_19-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFModriMatteoni2020">Modri &amp; Matteoni 2020</a>, p.&#160;5–6:Kvartiri, Croatia. A small stone house by the side of the road, the last one before the rocky slopes of the Velebit mountains. Six and a half kilometres from my parents' home in Zaton Obrovaki. This house was the centre of my little world until 1991, when we had to run away. This is where my father's parents lived: Grandpa Luka and Grandma Jela. My grandfather was a road mender, who maintained the old state road that connected Dalmatia and Lika, the coast and the mountains of Croatia. My grandmother was a housekeeper, a hardworking and modest woman. The house they lived in was owned by the road maintenance company, but back then I knew it only as my grandparents' home. We called it the 'upper house'. I never met my other grandfather, Petar, my mothers's father. He died before I was born. His wife, Grandma Manda, still lives in Obrovac. My parents worked at Trio Clothes Factory in Obrovac, four kilometres from our house. That's where they met.</span>
</li>
